pipeline:\n    1. Analyze intent/sentiment\n    2. Generate embedding\n    3. Save to database\n    4. Generate response\n    5. Return TTS audio\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        conn = get_db()\n        cur = conn.cursor()\n        \n        # Simple intent detection\n        text_lower = text.lower()\n        if any(w in text_lower for w in [\"navigate\", \"go to\", \"open\", \"show\"]):\n            intent = \"navigation\"\n        elif any(w in text_lower for w in [\"search\", \"find\", \"look for\"]):\n            intent = \"query\"\n        elif any(w in text_lower for w in [\"stop\", \"cancel\", \"close\"]):\n            intent = \"control\"\n        else:\n            intent = \"general\"\n        \n        # Simple sentiment\n        if any(w in text_lower for w in [\"great\", \"good\", \"awesome\", \"thanks\"]):\n            sentiment = \"positive\"\n        elif any(w in text_lower for w in [\"bad\", \"wrong\", \"error\", \"hate\"]):\n            sentiment = \"negative\"\n        else:\n            sentiment = \"neutral\"\n        \n        # Generate embedding\n        embedding = None\n        if embedding_model:\n            embedding = embedding_model.encode(text).tolist()\n        \n        # Save to database\n        cur.execute(\"\"\"\n            INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger \n            (user_type, raw_transcript, intent, sentiment, page_route, created_at)\n            VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, %s, NOW())\n            RETURNING id\n        \"\"\", (user_type, text, intent, sentiment, page_route))\n        ledger_id = cur.fetchone()[0]\n        \n        # Save to boss_commands with embedding\n        if embedding:\n            cur.execute(\"\"\"\n                INSERT INTO boss_commands \n                (raw_transcript, intent, page_context, embedding, created_at)\n                VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, NOW())\n                RETURNING id\n            \"\"\", (text, intent, page_route, embedding))\n        \n        # Update learned patterns\n        cur.execute(\"\"\"\n            INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count, last_seen)\n            VALUES (%s, %s, 1, NOW())\n            ON CONFLICT (pattern_text) \n            DO UPDATE SET occurrence_count = learned_patterns.occurrence_count + 1, last_seen = NOW()\n        \"\"\", (text.lower()[:100], intent))\n        \n        conn.commit()\n        cur.close()\n        conn.close()\n        \n        # Generate response based on intent\n        responses = {\n            \"navigation\": f\"Navigating you there right now, boss!\",\n            \"query\": f\"Let me search for that information.\",\n            \"control\": f\"Done! Action completed.\",\n            \"general\": f\"Got it! I'm processing your request.\"\n        }\n        response_text = responses.get(intent, \"I hear you, boss!\")\n        \n        return {\n            \"success\": True,\n            \"ledger_id\": ledger_id,\n            \"analysis\": {\n                \"intent\": intent,\n                \"sentiment\": sentiment,\n                \"hasEmbedding\": embedding is not None\n            },\n            \"response\": {\n                \"text\": response_text,\n                \"tone\": \"friendly\"\n            }\n        }\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        return JSONResponse(\n 'UTILSFILE'\n/**\n * Utility functions for signin components\n * Voice functionality is in src/hooks/useVoice.ts\n */\n\nexport function formatPhoneNumber(phone: string): string {\n    if (!phone) return '';\n    const cleaned = phone.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    if (cleaned.length === 10) {\n        return `(${cleaned.slice(0, 3)}) ${cleaned.slice(3, 6)}-${cleaned.slice(6)}`;\n    }\n    if (cleaned.length === 11) {\n        return `+${cleaned[0]} (${cleaned.slice(1, 4)}) ${cleaned.slice(4, 7)}-${cleaned.slice(7)}`;\n    }\n    return phone;\n}\n\nexport function speakablePhone(phone: string): string {\n    const cleaned = phone.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    return cleaned.split('').join(' ');\n}\n\nexport function validatePhoneNumber(phone: string): boolean {\n    const cleaned = phone.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    return cleaned.length >= 10 && cleaned.length <= 11;\n}\n\nexport function validateEmail(email: string): boolean {\n    return /^[^\\s@]+@[^\\s@]+\\.[^\\s@]+$/.test(email);\n}\n\nexport function formatCurrency(amount: number, currency: string = 'USD'): string {\n    return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', { style: 'currency', currency }).format(amount);\n}\n\nexport function debounce<T extends (...args: any[]) => any>(func: T, wait: number) {\n    let timeout: NodeJS.Timeout;\n    return (...args: Parameters<T>) => {\n        clearTimeout(timeout);\n        timeout = setTimeout(() => func(...args), wait);\n    };\n}\n\nexport function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {\n    return new Promise(resolve => \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\ntype VoiceState = 'idle' | 'listening' | 'processing' | 'speaking' | 'error';\n\ninterface VoiceOptions {\n    userType?: 'boss' | 'team' | 'user';\n    autoStart?: boolean;\n    onTranscript?: (text: string, isFinal: boolean) => void;\n    onResponse?: (data: any) => void;\n    onStateChange?: (state: VoiceState) => void;\n}\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// GLOBAL SINGLETON - Shared across ALL components\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\nlet globalRecognition: SpeechRecognition | null = null;\nlet globalIsActive = false;\nlet globalListeners: Set<(transcript: string) => void> = new Set();\nlet initAttempted = false;\n\nfunction initGlobalRecognition() {\n    if (initAttempted) return;\n    initAttempted = true;\n    \n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\n    \n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (!SR) {\n        console.warn('[Voice] Speech recognition not supported');\n        return;\n    }\n    \n    globalRecognition = new SR();\n    globalRecognition.continuous = true;\n    globalRecognition.interimResults = true;\n    globalRecognition.lang = 'en-US';\n    \n    console.log('[Voice] \u2705 Global singleton initialized');\n}\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// THE HOOK\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\nexport function useVoice(options: VoiceOptions = {}) {\n    const [state, setState] = useState<VoiceState>('idle');\n    const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n    const [interimTranscript, setInterimTranscript] = useState('');\n    const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);\n    \n    const shouldRunRef = useRef(false);\n    const restartTimeoutRef = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout | null>(null);\n    const isSpeakingRef = useRef(false);\n    const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\n    const optionsRef = useRef(options);\n    \n    // Keep options ref updated\n    useEffect(() => {\n        optionsRef.current = options;\n    }, [options]);\n    \n    // Initialize\n    useEffect(() => {\n        initGlobalRecognition();\n        synthRef.current = typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.speechSynthesis : null;\n        \n        return () => {\n            if (restartTimeoutRef.current) {\n                clearTimeout(restartTimeoutRef.current);\n            }\n        };\n    }, []);\n    \n    // Setup event handlers\n    useEffect(() => {\n        if (!globalRecognition) return;\n        \n        const handleStart = () => {\n            console.log('[Voice] \ud83c\udfa4 Listening');\n            globalIsActive = true;\n            setState('listening');\n            optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('listening');\n        };\n        \n        const handleResult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\n            let interim = '';\n            let final = '';\n            \n            for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\n                const t = event.results[i][0].transcript;\n                if (event.results[i].isFinal) {\n                    final += t;\n                } else {\n                    interim += t;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            setInterimTranscript(interim);\n            \n            if (final.trim()) {\n                console.log('[Voice] \ud83d\udcdd Final:', final.trim());\n                setTranscript(final.trim());\n                optionsRef.current.onTranscript?.(final.trim(), true);\n                processVoiceInput(final.trim());\n            }\n        };\n        \n        const handleError = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\n            // IGNORE these harmless errors completely\n            if (event.error === 'aborted' || event.error === 'no-speech') {\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            console.error('[Voice] \u274c', event.error);\n            \n            if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\n                setError('Microphone access denied');\n                setState('error');\n                shouldRunRef.current = false;\n            }\n        };\n        \n        const handleEnd = () => {\n            console.log('[Voice] \u23f9\ufe0f Ended');\n            globalIsActive = false;\n            \n            // Only restart if should be running AND not speaking\n            if (shouldRunRef.current && !isSpeakingRef.current) {\n                // Clear existing timeout\n                if (restartTimeoutRef.current) {\n                    clearTimeout(restartTimeoutRef.current);\n                }\n                \n                // LONG delay before restart - prevents loop\n                restartTimeoutRef.current = setTimeout(() => {\n                    if (shouldRunRef.current && !globalIsActive && !isSpeakingRef.current) {\n                        console.log('[Voice] \ud83d\udd04 Restarting after delay');\n                        safeStart();\n                    }\n                }, 1000); // 1 second delay\n            } else {\n                setState('idle');\n                optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('idle');\n            }\n        };\n        \n        globalRecognition.onstart = handleStart;\n        globalRecognition.onresult = handleResult;\n        globalRecognition.onerror = handleError;\n        globalRecognition.onend = handleEnd;\n        \n    }, []);\n    \n    // Safe start that prevents \"already started\" errors\n    const safeStart = useCallback(() => {\n        if (!globalRecognition || globalIsActive) return;\n        \n        try {\n            globalRecognition.start();\n        } catch (e: any) {\n            // Silently ignore \"already started\" errors\n            if (!e.message?.includes('already started')) {\n                console.error('[Voice] Start error:', e);\n            }\n        }\n    }, []);\n    \n    // Process voice input - send to backends\n    const processVoiceInput = useCallback(async (text: string) => {\n        console.log('[Voice] \ud83d\udce4 Processing:', text);\n        setState('processing');\n        optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('processing');\n        \n        try {\n            // Try Python Voice API first (has embeddings)\n            let response;\n            try {\n                response = await fetch('http://localhost:8000/process', {\n                    method: 'POST',\n                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' },\n                    body: new URLSearchParams({\n                        text,\n                        user_type: optionsRef.current.userType || 'boss',\n                        page_route: window.location.pathname\n                    })\n                });\n            } catch {\n                // Fallback to Node backend\n                response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/ledger/log', {\n                    method: 'POST',\n                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({\n                        user_type: optionsRef.current.userType || 'boss',\n                        raw_transcript: text,\n                        page_route: window.location.pathname\n                    })\n                });\n            }\n            \n            const data = await response.json();\n            console.log('[Voice] \ud83d\udce5 Response:', data);\n            \n            optionsRef.current.onResponse?.(data);\n            \n            // Speak response if available\n            const responseText = data?.response?.text || data?.tts_response?.text;\n            if (responseText) {\n                speak(responseText);\n            } else {\n                // Resume listening\n                if (shouldRunRef.current) {\n                    setState('listening');\n                } else {\n                    setState('idle');\n                }\n            }\n            \n        } catch (err: any) {\n            console.error('[Voice] Process error:', err);\n            setError(err.message);\n            setState(shouldRunRef.current ? 'listening' : 'idle');\n        }\n    }, []);\n    \n    // Start listening\n    const start = useCallback(() => {\n        console.log('[Voice] \u25b6\ufe0f Start');\n        \n        // Cancel any TTS\n        synthRef.current?.cancel();\n        isSpeakingRef.current = false;\n        \n        shouldRunRef.current = true;\n        setError(null);\n        \n        safeStart();\n    }, [safeStart]);\n    \n    // Stop listening\n    const stop = useCallback(() => {\n        console.log('[Voice] \u23f9\ufe0f Stop');\n        \n        shouldRunRef.current = false;\n        \n        if (restartTimeoutRef.current) {\n            clearTimeout(restartTimeoutRef.current);\n            restartTimeoutRef.current = null;\n        }\n        \n        if (globalRecognition && globalIsActive) {\n            try {\n                globalRecognition.stop();\n            } catch {}\n        }\n        \n        setState('idle');\n        optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('idle');\n    }, []);\n    \n    // Toggle\n    const toggle = useCallback(() => {\n        if (shouldRunRef.current || state === 'listening') {\n            stop();\n        } else {\n            start();\n        }\n    }, [state, start, stop]);\n    \n    // Speak with TTS (duplex - pauses STT)\n    const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\n        if (!synthRef.current) return;\n        \n        console.log('[Voice] \ud83d\udd0a Speaking:', text.substring(0, 40));\n        \n        const wasRunning = shouldRunRef.current;\n        \n        // Pause STT while speaking\n        isSpeakingRef.current = true;\n        if (globalIsActive && globalRecognition) {\n            try {\n                globalRecognition.stop();\n            } catch {}\n        }\n        \n        synthRef.current.cancel();\n        setState('speaking');\n        optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('speaking');\n        \n        const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n        utterance.rate = 0.95;\n        \n        utterance.onend = () => {\n            console.log('[Voice] \ud83d\udd0a Done speaking');\n            isSpeakingRef.current = false;\n            setState('idle');\n            \n            // Resume STT after speaking\n            if (wasRunning) {\n                shouldRunRef.current = true;\n                setTimeout(() => safeStart(), 500);\n            }\n        };\n        \n        utterance.onerror = () => {\n            isSpeakingRef.current = false;\n            setState('idle');\n            if (wasRunning) {\n                shouldRunRef.current = true;\n                setTimeout(() => safeStart(), 500);\n            }\n        };\n        \n        synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\n    }, [safeStart]);\n    \n    // Stop speaking\n    const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => {\n        synthRef.current?.cancel();\n        isSpeakingRef.current = false;\n        setState('idle');\n    }, []);\n    \n    return {\n        // State\n        state,\n        transcript,\n        interimTranscript,\n        error,\n        \n        // Computed\n        isListening: state === 'listening',\n        isSpeaking: state === 'speaking',\n        isProcessing: state === 'processing',\n        isIdle: state === 'idle',\n        isError: state === 'error',\n        \n        // Actions\n        start,\n        stop,\n        toggle,\n        speak,\n        stopSpeaking,\n        processVoiceInput\n    };\n}\n\nexport default useVoice;\nMAINVOICE\n\necho \"  \u2705 Created src/hooks/useVoice.ts (THE ONLY ONE)\"\n\n#\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n# 'AGENTICBAR'\n/**\n * \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n * VISTAVIEW AGENTIC BAR - Universal Voice Interface\n * \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n */\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';\nimport { useVoice } from '../../hooks/useVoice';\n\ninterface AgenticBarProps {\n    mode?: 'floating' | 'inline' | 'minimal';\n    position?: 'bottom' | 'top' | 'left' | 'right';\n    userType?: 'boss' | 'team' | 'user';\n    showTranscript?: boolean;\n    onCommand?: (text: string, response: any) => void;\n}\n\nexport function AgenticBar({\n    mode = 'floating',\n    position = 'bottom',\n    userType = 'boss',\n    showTranscript = true,\n    onCommand\n}: AgenticBarProps) {\n    const [lastResponse, setLastResponse] = useState<string>('');\n    \n    const {\n        state,\n        transcript,\n        interimTranscript,\n        isListening,\n        isSpeaking,\n        isProcessing,\n        start,\n        stop,\n        toggle,\n        speak\n    } = useVoice({\n        userType,\n        onResponse: (data) => {\n            const responseText = data?.response?.text || data?.tts_response?.text || '';\n            setLastResponse(responseText);\n            onCommand?.(transcript, data);\n        }\n    });\n    \n    // Keyboard shortcut: Space to toggle (when focused)\n    useEffect(() => {\n        const handleKeyDown = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {\n            if (e.code === 'Space' && e.target === document.body) {\n                e.preventDefault();\n                toggle();\n            }\n        };\n        \n        window.addEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);\n        return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);\n    }, [toggle]);\n    \n    // Status colors\n    const statusColors = {\n        idle: 'bg-gray-500',\n        listening: 'bg-green-500 animate-pulse',\n        processing: 'bg-yellow-500 animate-spin',\n        speaking: 'bg-blue-500 animate-pulse',\n        error: 'bg-red-500'\n    };\n    \n    // Position styles\n    const positionStyles = {\n        bottom: 'bottom-4 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2',\n        top: 'top-4 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2',\n        left: 'left-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2',\n        right: 'right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2'\n    };\n    \n    if (mode === 'minimal') {\n        return (\n            <button\n                onClick={toggle}\n                className={`w-12 h-12 rounded-full ${statusColors[state]} text-white flex items-center justify-center shadow-lg transition-all`}\n                title={isListening ? 'Stop listening' : 'Start listening'}\n            >\n                {isListening ? '\ud83c\udfa4' : '\ud83c\udf99\ufe0f'}\n            </button>\n        );\n    }\n    \n    return (\n        <div className={`fixed ${positionStyles[position]} z-50`}>\n            <div className=\"bg-gray-900 rounded-2xl shadow-2xl p-4 min-w-[300px] border border-gray-700\">\n                {/* Header */}\n                <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between mb-3\">\n                    <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n                        <div className={`w-3 h-3 rounded-full ${statusColors[state]}`} />\n                        <span className=\"text-white text-sm font-medium\">\n                            {state === 'listening' && 'Listening...'}\n                            {state === 'processing' && 'Processing...'}\n                            {state === 'speaking' && 'Speaking...'}\n                            {state === 'idle' && 'Ready'}\n                            {state === 'error' && 'Error'}\n                        </span>\n                    </div>\n                    <span className=\"text-gray-400 text-xs\">\n                        {userType === 'boss' ? '\ud83d\udc54 Boss' : '\ud83d\udc64 User'}\n                    </span>\n                </div>\n                \n                {/* Transcript Display */}\n                {showTranscript && (\n                    <div className=\"bg-gray-800 rounded-lg p-3 mb-3 min-h-[60px]\">\n                        {interimTranscript && (\n                            <p className=\"text-gray-400 text-sm italic\">{interimTranscript}</p>\n                        )}\n                        {transcript && (\n                            <p className=\"text-white text-sm\">{transcript}</p>\n                        )}\n                        {lastResponse && (\n                            <p className=\"text-green-400 text-sm mt-2\">\u2192 {lastResponse}</p>\n                        )}\n                        {!transcript && !interimTranscript && !lastResponse && (\n                            <p className=\"text-gray-500 text-sm\">Say something...</p>\n                        )}\n                    </div>\n                )}\n                \n                {/* Controls */}\n                <div className=\"flex items-center justify-center gap-3\">\n                    <button\n                        onClick={toggle}\n                        className={`w-14 h-14 rounded-full ${\n                            isListening ? 'bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600' : 'bg-green-500 hover:bg-green-600'\n                        } text-white text-2xl flex items-center justify-center transition-all shadow-lg`}\n                    >\n                        {isListening ? }\\n\\n@app.post(\\\"/process\\\")\\nasync def process_voice(\\n    text: str,\\n    user_type: str = \\\"boss\\\",\\n    page_route: str = \\\"/\\\"\\n):\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    Full voice processing pipeline:\\n    1. Analyze intent/sentiment\\n    2. Generate embedding\\n    3. Save to database\\n    4. Generate response\\n    5. Return TTS audio\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    try:\\n        conn = get_db()\\n        cur = conn.cursor()\\n        \\n        # Simple intent detection\\n        text_lower = text.lower()\\n        if any(w in text_lower for w in [\\\"navigate\\\", \\\"go to\\\", \\\"open\\\", \\\"show\\\"]):\\n            intent = \\\"navigation\\\"\\n        elif any(w in text_lower for w in [\\\"search\\\", \\\"find\\\", \\\"look for\\\"]):\\n            intent = \\\"query\\\"\\n        elif any(w in text_lower for w in [\\\"stop\\\", \\\"cancel\\\", \\\"close\\\"]):\\n            intent = \\\"control\\\"\\n        else:\\n            intent = \\\"general\\\"\\n        \\n        # embedding is not None\\n            },\\n            \\\"response\\\": {\\n                \\\"text\\\": response_text,\\n                \\\"tone\\\": \\\"friendly\\\"\\n            }\\n        }\\n        \\n    except Exception as e:\\n        return JSONResponse(\\n            status_code=500,\\n            content={\\\"success\\\": False, \\\"error\\\": str(e)}\\n        )\\n\\nif __name__ == formatPhoneNumber(phone: string): string {\\n    if (!phone) return '';\\n    const cleaned = phone.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    if (cleaned.length === 10) {\\n        return `(${cleaned.slice(0, 3)}) ${cleaned.slice(3, 6)}-${cleaned.slice(6)}`;\\n    }\\n    if (cleaned.length === 11) {\\n        return `+${cleaned[0]} (${cleaned.slice(1, 4)}) ${cleaned.slice(4, 7)}-${cleaned.slice(7)}`;\\n    }\\n    return phone;\\n}\\n\\nexport function speakablePhone(phone: string): string {\\n    const cleaned = phone.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    return cleaned.split('').join(' ');\\n}\\n\\nexport \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\ntype VoiceState = 'idle' | 'listening' | 'processing' | 'speaking' | 'error';\\n\\ninterface VoiceOptions {\\n    userType?: 'boss' | 'team' | 'user';\\n    autoStart?: boolean;\\n    onTranscript?: (text: string, isFinal: boolean) => void;\\n    onResponse?: (data: any) => void;\\n    onStateChange?: (state: VoiceState) => void;\\n}\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// GLOBAL SINGLETON - Shared across ALL components\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\nlet globalRecognition: SpeechRecognition | null = null;\\nlet globalIsActive = false;\\nlet globalListeners: Set<(transcript: string) => void> = new Set();\\nlet initAttempted = false;\\n\\nfunction initGlobalRecognition() {\\n    if (initAttempted) return;\\n    initAttempted = true;\\n    \\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\\n    \\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (!SR) {\\n        console.warn('[Voice] Speech recognition not supported');\\n        return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    globalRecognition = new SR();\\n    globalRecognition.continuous = true;\\n    globalRecognition.interimResults = true;\\n    globalRecognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n    \\n    console.log('[Voice] \\u2705 Global singleton initialized');\\n}\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// THE HOOK\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\nexport function useVoice(options: VoiceOptions = {}) {\\n    const [state, setState] = useState<VoiceState>('idle');\\n    const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n    const [interimTranscript, setInterimTranscript] = useState('');\\n    const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);\\n    \\n    const shouldRunRef = useRef(false);\\n    const restartTimeoutRef = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout | null>(null);\\n    const isSpeakingRef = useRef(false);\\n    const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\\n    const optionsRef = useRef(options);\\n    \\n    // Keep options ref updated\\n    useEffect(() => {\\n        optionsRef.current = options;\\n    }, [options]);\\n    \\n    // Initialize\\n    useEffect(() => {\\n        initGlobalRecognition();\\n        synthRef.current = typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.speechSynthesis : null;\\n        \\n        return () => {\\n            if (restartTimeoutRef.current) {\\n                clearTimeout(restartTimeoutRef.current);\\n            }\\n        };\\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    // Setup event handlers\\n    useEffect(() => {\\n        if (!globalRecognition) return;\\n        \\n        const handleStart = () => {\\n            console.log('[Voice] \\ud83c\\udfa4 Listening');\\n            globalIsActive = true;\\n            setState('listening');\\n            optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('listening');\\n        };\\n        \\n        const handleResult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n            let interim = '';\\n            let final = '';\\n            \\n            for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\\n                const t = event.results[i][0].transcript;\\n                if (event.results[i].isFinal) {\\n                    final += t;\\n                } else {\\n                    interim += t;\\n                }\\n            }\\n            \\n            setInterimTranscript(interim);\\n            \\n            if (final.trim()) {\\n                console.log('[Voice] \\ud83d\\udcdd Final:', final.trim());\\n                setTranscript(final.trim());\\n                optionsRef.current.onTranscript?.(final.trim(), true);\\n                processVoiceInput(final.trim());\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        const handleError = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n            // IGNORE these harmless errors completely\\n            if (event.error === 'aborted' || event.error === 'no-speech') {\\n                return;\\n            }\\n            \\n            console.error('[Voice] \\u274c', event.error);\\n            \\n            if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n                setError('Microphone access denied');\\n                setState('error');\\n                shouldRunRef.current = false;\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        const handleEnd = () => {\\n            console.log('[Voice] \\u23f9\\ufe0f Ended');\\n            globalIsActive = false;\\n            \\n            // Only restart if should be running AND not speaking\\n            if (shouldRunRef.current && !isSpeakingRef.current) {\\n                // Clear existing timeout\\n                if (restartTimeoutRef.current) {\\n                    clearTimeout(restartTimeoutRef.current);\\n                }\\n                \\n                // LONG delay before restart - prevents loop\\n                restartTimeoutRef.current = setTimeout(() => {\\n                    if (shouldRunRef.current && !globalIsActive && !isSpeakingRef.current) {\\n                        console.log('[Voice] \\ud83d\\udd04 Restarting after delay');\\n                        safeStart();\\n                    }\\n                }, 1000); // 1 second delay\\n            } else {\\n                setState('idle');\\n                optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('idle');\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        globalRecognition.onstart = handleStart;\\n        globalRecognition.onresult = handleResult;\\n        globalRecognition.onerror = handleError;\\n        globalRecognition.onend = handleEnd;\\n        \\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    // Safe start that prevents \\\"already started\\\" errors\\n    const safeStart = useCallback(() => {\\n        if (!globalRecognition || globalIsActive) return;\\n        \\n        try {\\n            globalRecognition.start();\\n        } catch (e: any) {\\n            // Silently ignore \\\"already started\\\" errors\\n            if (!e.message?.includes('already started')) {\\n                console.error('[Voice] Start error:', e);\\n            }\\n        }\\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    // Process voice input - send to backends\\n    const processVoiceInput = useCallback(async (text: string) => {\\n        console.log('[Voice] \\ud83d\\udce4 Processing:', text);\\n        setState('processing');\\n        optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('processing');\\n        \\n        try {\\n            // Try Python Voice API first (has embeddings)\\n            let response;\\n            try {\\n                response = await fetch('http://localhost:8000/process', {\\n                    method: 'POST',\\n                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' },\\n                    body: new URLSearchParams({\\n                        text,\\n                        user_type: optionsRef.current.userType || 'boss',\\n                        page_route: window.location.pathname\\n                    })\\n                });\\n            } catch {\\n                // Fallback to Node backend\\n                response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/ledger/log', {\\n                    method: 'POST',\\n                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n                    body: JSON.stringify({\\n                        user_type: optionsRef.current.userType || 'boss',\\n                        raw_transcript: text,\\n                        page_route: window.location.pathname\\n                    })\\n                });\\n            }\\n            \\n            const data = await response.json();\\n            console.log('[Voice] \\ud83d\\udce5 Response:', data);\\n            \\n            optionsRef.current.onResponse?.(data);\\n            \\n            // Speak response if available\\n            const responseText = data?.response?.text || data?.tts_response?.text;\\n            if (responseText) {\\n                speak(responseText);\\n            } else {\\n                // Resume listening\\n                if (shouldRunRef.current) {\\n                    setState('listening');\\n                } else {\\n                    setState('idle');\\n                }\\n            }\\n            \\n        } catch (err: any) {\\n            console.error('[Voice] Process error:', err);\\n            setError(err.message);\\n            setState(shouldRunRef.current ? 'listening' : 'idle');\\n        }\\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    // Start listening\\n    const start = useCallback(() => {\\n        console.log('[Voice] \\u25b6\\ufe0f Start');\\n        \\n        // Cancel any TTS\\n        synthRef.current?.cancel();\\n        isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n        \\n        shouldRunRef.current = true;\\n        setError(null);\\n        \\n        safeStart();\\n    }, [safeStart]);\\n    \\n    // Stop listening\\n    const stop = useCallback(() => {\\n        console.log('[Voice] \\u23f9\\ufe0f Stop');\\n        \\n        shouldRunRef.current = false;\\n        \\n        if (restartTimeoutRef.current) {\\n            clearTimeout(restartTimeoutRef.current);\\n            restartTimeoutRef.current = null;\\n        }\\n        \\n        if (globalRecognition && globalIsActive) {\\n            try {\\n                globalRecognition.stop();\\n            } catch {}\\n        }\\n        \\n        setState('idle');\\n        optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('idle');\\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    // Toggle\\n    const toggle = useCallback(() => {\\n        if (shouldRunRef.current || state === 'listening') {\\n            stop();\\n        } else {\\n            start();\\n        }\\n    }, [state, start, stop]);\\n    \\n    // Speak with TTS (duplex - pauses STT)\\n    const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n        if (!synthRef.current) return;\\n        \\n        console.log('[Voice] \\ud83d\\udd0a Speaking:', text.substring(0, 40));\\n        \\n        const wasRunning = shouldRunRef.current;\\n        \\n        // Pause STT while speaking\\n        isSpeakingRef.current = true;\\n        if (globalIsActive && globalRecognition) {\\n            try {\\n                globalRecognition.stop();\\n            } catch {}\\n        }\\n        \\n        synthRef.current.cancel();\\n        setState('speaking');\\n        optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('speaking');\\n        \\n        const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n        utterance.rate = 0.95;\\n        \\n        utterance.onend = () => {\\n            console.log('[Voice] \\ud83d\\udd0a Done speaking');\\n            isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n            setState('idle');\\n            \\n            // Resume STT after speaking\\n            if (wasRunning) {\\n                shouldRunRef.current = true;\\n                setTimeout(() => safeStart(), 500);\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        utterance.onerror = () => {\\n            isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n            setState('idle');\\n            if (wasRunning) {\\n                shouldRunRef.current = true;\\n                setTimeout(() => safeStart(), 500);\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\\n    }, [safeStart]);\\n    \\n    // Stop speaking\\n    const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => {\\n        synthRef.current?.cancel();\\n        isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n        setState('idle');\\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    return {\\n        // State\\n        state,\\n        transcript,\\n        interimTranscript,\\n        error,\\n        \\n        // Computed\\n        isListening: state === 'listening',\\n        isSpeaking: state === 'speaking',\\n        isProcessing: state === 'processing',\\n        isIdle: state === 'idle',\\n        isError: state === 'error',\\n        \\n        // Actions\\n        start,\\n        stop,\\n        toggle,\\n        speak,\\n        stopSpeaking,\\n        processVoiceInput\\n    };\\n}\\n\\nexport default useVoice;\\nMAINVOICE\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 Created src/hooks/useVoice.ts (THE ONLY ONE)\\\"\\n\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n# STEP 4: CREATE UNIFIED AGENTIC BAR COMPONENT\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\necho \\\"$VV/src/components/common/AgenticBar.tsx\\\" << 'AGENTICBAR'\\n/**\\n * \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n * VISTAVIEW AGENTIC BAR - Universal Voice Interface\\n * \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n * \\n * Use this component on ANY page for consistent voice experience.\\n * \\n * Usage:\\n *   import { AgenticBar } from '@/components/common/AgenticBar';\\n *   <AgenticBar mode=\\\"floating\\\" />\\n */\\n\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';\\nimport { useVoice } from '../../hooks/useVoice';\\n\\ninterface AgenticBarProps {\\n    mode?: 'floating' | 'inline' | 'minimal';\\n    position?: 'bottom' | 'top' | 'left' | 'right';\\n    userType?: 'boss' | 'team' | 'user';\\n    showTranscript?: boolean;\\n    onCommand?: (text: string, response: any) => void;\\n}\\n\\nexport function AgenticBar({\\n    mode = 'floating',\\n    position = 'bottom',\\n    userType = 'boss',\\n    showTranscript = true,\\n    onCommand\\n}: AgenticBarProps) {\\n    const [lastResponse, setLastResponse] = useState<string>('');\\n    \\n    const {\\n        state,\\n        transcript,\\n        interimTranscript,\\n        isListening,\\n        isSpeaking,\\n        isProcessing,\\n        start,\\n        stop,\\n        toggle,\\n        speak\\n    } = useVoice({\\n        userType,\\n        onResponse: (data) => {\\n            const responseText = data?.response?.text || data?.tts_response?.text || '';\\n            setLastResponse(responseText);\\n            onCommand?.(transcript, data);\\n        }\\n    });\\n    \\n    // Keyboard shortcut: Space to toggle (when focused)\\n    useEffect(() => {\\n        const handleKeyDown = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {\\n            if (e.code === 'Space' && e.target === document.body) {\\n                e.preventDefault();\\n                toggle();\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        window.addEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);\\n        return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);\\n    }, [toggle]);\\n    \\n    // Status colors\\n    const statusColors = {\\n        idle: 'bg-gray-500',\\n        listening: 'bg-green-500 animate-pulse',\\n        processing: 'bg-yellow-500 animate-spin',\\n        speaking: 'bg-blue-500 animate-pulse',\\n        error: 'bg-red-500'\\n    };\\n    \\n    // Position styles\\n    const positionStyles = {\\n        bottom: 'bottom-4 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2',\\n        top: 'top-4 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2',\\n        left: 'left-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2',\\n        right: 'right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2'\\n    };\\n    \\n    if (mode === 'minimal') {\\n        return (\\n            <button\\n                onClick={toggle}\\n                className={`w-12 h-12 rounded-full ${statusColors[state]} text-white flex items-center justify-center shadow-lg transition-all`}\\n                title={isListening ? 'Stop listening' : 'Start listening'}\\n            >\\n                {isListening ?
